<p><img src="assets/images/image-20251228-b28d71b7.jpeg" alt="img-8.jpeg"></p>
<p>"I remember the face but I've forgotten your name."</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="incidence">Incidence<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#incidence" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Is more common in elderly than middle aged.</li>
<li>Increases with age from 0.1% from those below 60 years to 15-20% to those who are 80 years.</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="etiology">ETIOLOGY<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#etiology" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ul>
<li>Significant loss of neurons and volume in brain regions devoted to memory and mental functioning.</li>
<li>Damage of the support structures of the nerve cells</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="cont">cont<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#cont" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Accumulation of beta amyloid, an insoluble protein which form sticky patches in neurons</li>
<li>Deficiencies of vitamin B6,B12 and folate</li>
<li>Infections of the nervous system like encephalitis</li>
<li>Serious head injuries.</li>
<li>Excessive metal ions like zinc in the body.</li>
</ul>
<p><img src="assets/images/image-20251228-3ec9de86.jpeg" alt="img-9.jpeg"></p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="untreatable-or-irreversible-forms-of-dementia">Untreatable or irreversible forms of dementia<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#untreatable-or-irreversible-forms-of-dementia" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Degenerating disorders of the CNS.</li>
<li>Huntington's chorea : a hereditary disease marked by progressive degeneration of nerve cells in the brain</li>
<li>Parkinson disease</li>
<li>Alzheimer's disease.</li>
<li>Picks disease</li>
</ul>
<p><img src="assets/images/image-20251228-f9dfeb34.jpeg" alt="img-10.jpeg"></p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="treatable-or-reversible-forms-of-dementia">Treatable or reversible forms of dementia<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#treatable-or-reversible-forms-of-dementia" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Vascular or multi-infact dementia</li>
<li>Dementia resulting from intracranial space occupying lesions</li>
<li>Dementia resulting from metabolic disorders like hepatic and renal failure.</li>
<li>Dementia resulting from endocrine disorders like Addison disease.</li>
<li>Dementia resulting from infections like AIDS, meningitis and encephalitis.</li>
<li>Dementia resulting from vitamin deficiency like thiamine</li>
<li>Dementia resulting from Anoxia</li>
</ul>
<p><img src="assets/images/image-20251228-c23db6a2.jpeg" alt="img-11.jpeg"></p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="stages-in-development-of-dementia">Stages in development of dementia<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#stages-in-development-of-dementia" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Dementia develops in three stages.</li>
</ul>
<ol>
<li>Stage one (2-4)</li>
</ol>
<ul>
<li>Develop between 2-4 years.</li>
<li>Characterized by:-</li>
<li>Forgetfulness</li>
<li>Declining interest in environment</li>
<li>Poor performance at work.</li>
</ul>
<ol start="2">
<li>Stage two: (2-12 yrs)</li>
</ol>
<p>Characterized by:-</p>
<ul>
<li>Progressive memory loss</li>
<li>Difficulty in following instructions</li>
<li>Hesitancy in response to questions</li>
<li>Irritable and anxious</li>
<li>Wandering</li>
<li>Neglect personal hygiene</li>
<li>Social isolation.</li>
</ul>
<p><img src="assets/images/image-20251228-3ec9de86.jpeg" alt="img-12.jpeg"></p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="stage-3-final-stage">Stage 3: Final stage<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#stage-3-final-stage" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Marked loss of weight because of inadequate intake of food.</li>
<li>Unable to communicate</li>
<li>Does not recognize family members</li>
<li>Incontinence of urine and feaces</li>
<li>Loss of ability to stand and walk</li>
</ul>
<p><img src="assets/images/image-20251228-f9dfeb34.jpeg" alt="img-13.jpeg"></p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="risk-factors-for-dementia">Risk factors for dementia<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#risk-factors-for-dementia" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Family history of Alzheimer's disease</li>
<li>Increased age</li>
<li>Head trauma</li>
<li>Cardiovascular diseases</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="investigations">INVESTIGATIONS<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#investigations" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ul>
<li>Full hemogram</li>
<li>UECs</li>
<li>CT scan and MRI</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="treatment-of-dementia">Treatment of dementia<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#treatment-of-dementia" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Treatment of any reversible cause: hydrocephalus, renal failure, hypothyroidism, brain lesions, subdural hematoma, Vit B6 and B12, folate deficiencies.</li>
<li>Pharmacologic treatment:</li>
<li>Tacrine (cognex), a cholinergic drug that improves cognitive functioning. However, its use is limited due to liver toxicity.</li>
<li>Antidepressants, antianxiety, and antipsychotics used to relieve associated symptoms like hallucinations and delusions.</li>
<li>Antiepileptic drugs for multi-infarct dementia</li>
<li>Benzodiazepines for insomnia and anxiety.</li>
</ul>
<p><img src="assets/images/image-20251228-3ec9de86.jpeg" alt="img-14.jpeg"></p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="nursing-management">Nursing management<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#nursing-management" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Assess the patient level of functioning to formulate appropriate plan of care.</li>
<li>Provide safety to the patient. Assess the patient level of disorientation to determine specific requirement for safety.</li>
<li>Maintain daily routines to include drawing up a fixed timetable for patient for waking up, toilet, exercise and meals,</li>
</ul>
<p>cont</p>
<ul>
<li>Provide additional care during evening due to sun downing. This is a situation where patient condition deteriorates during evening and additional care must be provided.</li>
<li>Orient the patient to reality in order to decrease confusion. use calendar with large writing and a separate page for each day. Provide newspapers which stimulate interest in events</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="cont">cont<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#cont" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Provide a well balance diet rich in protein, higher fiber with adequate amount of calories. Allow plenty of time for meals.</li>
<li>Provide daily personal hygiene to include brushing of teeth, bathing, keeping the skin clean and dry.</li>
<li>Provide toilet habits and maintained it as a rigid routine. The patient should be taken to urinate at a fixed interval depending on fluid intake and season</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="cont">cont<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#cont" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Prevent accidents from falling, slipping in bathroom and tripping over furniture by providing patients with firmly secured shoes. Any floor covering must be firmly secured.</li>
<li>Decrease the amount of stimuli to the patient environment so that confusion may be less.</li>
<li>Help the patient devise methods to reduce memory defects e.g. by asking them to note down the daily activities.</li>
</ul>
<p>cont</p>
<ul>
<li>Use simple explanations and face to face introduction and communication to the patient.</li>
<li>Provided sufficient fluid during the day and minimum amount of fluid at evening around 6pm</li>
<li>Keep calm environment with fixed schedules to prevent changes in mood which are unpredictable.</li>
<li>Provide identification tag for patients with Alzheimer's disease as they are prone to wandering due to disorientation</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="multi-infarct-dementia">Multi-infarct dementia<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#multi-infarct-dementia" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Condition characterized by an alteration in due brain function due to destruction of brain tissues</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="contributing-factors">Contributing factors<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#contributing-factors" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ul>
<li>Advanced age</li>
<li>Cerebral emboli or thrombosis</li>
<li>Diabetes</li>
<li>Heart disease</li>
<li>High blood cholesterol</li>
<li>Hypertension</li>
</ul>
<p><img src="assets/images/image-20251228-97cd6855.jpeg" alt="img-15.jpeg"></p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="signs-and-symptoms">Signs and symptoms<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#signs-and-symptoms" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Confusion</li>
<li>Wandering or getting lost in familiar places</li>
<li>Leg or arm weakness</li>
<li>Problems with recent memory</li>
<li>Loss of bladder and bowel control</li>
<li>Inappropriate emotional reaction such as laughing or crying inappropriately</li>
<li>Problems with recent memory</li>
<li>Difficulty in following instructions</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="nursing-interventions">Nursing interventions<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#nursing-interventions" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Reduce unnecessary stimulation</li>
<li>Avoid changing patient room and moving furniture</li>
<li>Orient patient to the surrounding</li>
<li>Make environment as stable as possible</li>
</ul>
<p><img src="assets/images/image-20251228-7a2f108f.jpeg" alt="img-16.jpeg"></p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="alzheimer-s-disease">Alzheimer's disease<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#alzheimer-s-disease" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="introduction">INTRODUCTION<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#introduction" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Alzheimer's disease is a degenerative brain disorder of unknown etiology which is the most common form of dementia</li>
<li>Usually starts in late middle age or in old age</li>
<li>Results in progressive memory loss, impaired thinking, disorientation, and changes in personality and mood.</li>
</ul>
<p><img src="assets/images/image-20251228-7efd2db1.jpeg" alt="img-17.jpeg"></p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="origin-of-alzheimer-s-disease">Origin of Alzheimer's Disease<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#origin-of-alzheimer-s-disease" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>The disease was first described by Dr. Alois Alzheimer, a German physician, in 1906. Alzheimer had a patient named Auguste D, in her fifties who suffered from what seemed to be a mental illness.</li>
<li>But when she died in 1906, an autopsy revealed dense deposits, now called neuritic plaques, outside and around the nerve cells in her brain. Inside the cells were twisted strands of fiber, or neurofibrillary tangles.</li>
<li>Since Dr. Alois Alzheimer's was the first person who discovered the disease, AD was named after him.</li>
</ul>
<p><img src="assets/images/image-20251228-2ee043cb.jpeg" alt="img-18.jpeg">
Auguste D</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="definition">Definition<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#definition" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Alzheimers disease is a chronic, <strong>irreversible</strong> disease that affects the cells of the brain and causes impairment of intellectual functioning.</li>
<li>Alzheimers disease is a brain disorder which gradually destroys the ability to reason, remember, imagine, and learn.</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="incidence">INCIDENCE<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#incidence" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>About 3 percent of men and women ages 65 to 74 have AD, and nearly half of those age 85 and older may have the disease.</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="causes">CAUSES<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#causes" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>The cause of Alzheimers disease is not known.</li>
<li>However, several factors are thought to be implicated in this disease e.g.</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="environmental-factors">ENVIRONMENTAL FACTORS<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#environmental-factors" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Cigarette smoking.</li>
<li>Certain Infections.</li>
<li>Metals, industrial or other toxins.</li>
<li>Use of cholesterol lowering drugs (statin).</li>
</ul>
<p><img src="assets/images/image-20251228-4308dbf8.jpeg" alt="img-19.jpeg"></p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="signs-of-alzheimer-s-disease">Signs of Alzheimer's disease<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#signs-of-alzheimer-s-disease" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<p>Ten warning signs of Alzheimer's disease</p>
<ol>
<li>Memory loss</li>
<li>Difficulty to performing familiar tasks</li>
<li>Problems with language</li>
<li>Disorientation to time and place</li>
<li>Poor or decreased judgment</li>
<li>Problems with abstract thinking</li>
<li>Misplacing things</li>
<li>Changes in mood or behavior</li>
<li>Changes in personality</li>
<li>Loss of initiative</li>
</ol>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="symptoms-of-alzheimer-s-disease">Symptoms of Alzheimer's disease<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#symptoms-of-alzheimer-s-disease" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Confusion</li>
<li>Disturbances in short-term memory</li>
<li>Problems with attention and spatial orientation</li>
<li>Personality changes</li>
<li>Language difficulties</li>
<li>Unexplained mood swings</li>
</ul>
<p><img src="assets/images/image-20251228-97cd6855.jpeg" alt="img-20.jpeg"></p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="delirium-acute-organic-syndrome">DELIRIUM (ACUTE ORGANIC SYNDROME)<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#delirium-acute-organic-syndrome" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Defn: Refers to acute organic mental disorder characterized by;</li>
<li>(i) Impairment of consciousness I.E. decreased awareness to surrounding</li>
<li>(ii) Disorientation, mostly time, but in severe cases, place and person</li>
<li>(iii) Disturbance in perception and restlessness. Has illusions and or hallucinations.</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="incidence">Incidence<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#incidence" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ul>
<li>Has the highest incidence among organic mental disorders.</li>
<li>Account for 10-25% of medical  surgical patients and about 20-40% of geriatric patients</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="causes-of-delirium">Causes of delirium<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#causes-of-delirium" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Endocrine and metabolic conditions like diabetic coma, uremia, hyperthyroidism and kidney failure</li>
<li>Thiamine deficiency</li>
<li>Traumatic events leading to: Subdural and epidural hematomas</li>
<li>Vascular problems cerebral arteriosclerosis</li>
<li>Infections like meningitis and encephalitis</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="cont">cont<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#cont" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Withdrawal effects of sedatives</li>
<li>Neoplasm : space occupying lesions</li>
<li>Anemia</li>
<li>Toxins in the brain</li>
</ul>
<p><img src="assets/images/image-20251228-3ec9de86.jpeg" alt="img-21.jpeg"></p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="signs-and-symptoms">Signs and symptoms<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#signs-and-symptoms" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Impairment of consciousness: clouding of consciousness ranging from stupor to coma</li>
<li>Clouding means loss of clarity ... it means lowered level of consciousness</li>
<li>Impairment in attention; difficulty in focusing and sustaining attention</li>
<li>Illusions and hallucinations esp visual</li>
<li>Loss of recent and immediate memory</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="cont">cont<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#cont" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Hypo activity or hyperactivity characterized by flocculation (aimless picking of bed clothes)</li>
<li>Disturbances in sleep pattern including insomnia, disturbing dreams or nightmares</li>
<li>Emotional disturbances including depression, anxiety, fear, irritability euphoria and apathy.</li>
</ul>
<p><img src="assets/images/image-20251228-7efd2db1.jpeg" alt="img-22.jpeg"></p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="course-and-prognosis">Course and prognosis<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#course-and-prognosis" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>It has abrupt onset</li>
<li>Duration of episode is brief lasting for about a week</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="treatment">TREATMENT<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#treatment" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ul>
<li>Identification of a cause and its immediate correction e.g. correction of hypoglycemia and vitamin deficiency.</li>
<li>Symptomatic treatment: <strong>Benzodiazepines</strong> e.g. lorazepam, Diazepam, and <strong>antipsychotics</strong> e.g. Haloperidol may be given</li>
</ul>
<p><img src="assets/images/image-20251228-3ec9de86.jpeg" alt="img-23.jpeg"></p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="nursing-management">Nursing management<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#nursing-management" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Provide safety of the patient as the patient is responding to hallucinatory illusions and delusions</li>
<li>Restrict environmental stimuli, keep the unit calm and well illuminated</li>
<li>Keep the room well lighted especially at night</li>
<li>Provide a caregiver at the bed side of the patient at all times to provide security</li>
</ul>
<p><img src="assets/images/image-20251228-7efd2db1.jpeg" alt="img-24.jpeg"></p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="cont">cont<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#cont" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Observe the patient for extreme drowsiness and sleep as it may indicate the patient into coma.</li>
<li>Reduce fever if present</li>
<li>Hydrate the patient and maintain intake and output</li>
<li>Monitor vitals signs</li>
<li>Orient the patient by :</li>
<li>Repeatedly explaining to the patient where he is and what date, day and time</li>
<li>Introduce people with names</li>
<li>Have a calendar in room and tell the patient what day it is</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="anxiety-disorders">ANXIETY DISORDERS<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#anxiety-disorders" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<p>OKEMWA</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="objectives">Objectives<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#objectives" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<p>By the end of the lesson, the learner should be able to:-</p>
<ul>
<li>Define anxiety</li>
<li>Differentiate between anxiety and fear</li>
<li>Theories explaining anxiety.</li>
<li>Describe the types of anxiety disorders in terms of criteria of diagnosis, signs and symptoms, factors associated with each and the management.</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="introduction">Introduction<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#introduction" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>
<p>Anxiety vs Fear</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Fear: acute, immediate response to suddenly appearing, imminent danger (proximal threats)</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Fear involves subjective feelings of apprehension and objective physiological changes such as rapid heart beat, muscle tremor etc in preparation for flight or fight tendencies.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Anxiety:</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>A sustained feeling of uneasiness and apprehension about some undefined threat either physical or psychological with threats to self-esteem, wellbeing or bodily harm.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Unlike fear, anxiety stems from sources that are not obvious or seems minor to the person who suffers.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="causes-of-anxiety">Causes of anxiety<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#causes-of-anxiety" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<p>Many theories exist since the advent of Freud's pioneering work identifying anxiety as a universal human emotion that directs human behaviour.</p>
<p>The cognitive model attributes anxiety to a disordered thinking (the cognitive triad)</p>
<p>Other causes of anxiety include: Dysfunctional beliefs/rules, Biological basis i.e. the limbic system</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="levels-of-anxiety">Levels of Anxiety<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#levels-of-anxiety" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Mild: adaptive day to day tension</li>
<li>Moderate: difficulty focusing with mild somatic complaints such as mild stomach upsets</li>
<li>Severe: unable to focus on problem solving, increased physical discomfort, direction needed to focus attention</li>
<li>Panic: awe, dread, terror, distortion of perception, disorganized personality</li>
</ul>
<p>Maladaptive coping to anxiety leads to Anxiety disorders with a common feature of anxiety:</p>
<ul>
<li>Generalized anxiety disorder</li>
<li>Selective mutism</li>
<li>Separation anxiety disorder</li>
<li>Specific phobia</li>
<li>Social anxiety disorder (social phobia)</li>
<li>Panic disorder</li>
<li>Agoraphobia</li>
<li>Substance/medication-Induced Anxiety Disorder.</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="generalized-anxiety-disorder">Generalized Anxiety Disorder<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#generalized-anxiety-disorder" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<p>This is an anxiety disorder characterized by excessive anxiety and worry occurring on most days for at least 6 months.</p>
<p>The anxiety is about a number of different events or activities and the individual finds it difficult to control.</p>
<p><img src="assets/images/image-20251228-de8de85b.jpeg" alt="img-25.jpeg"></p>
<p>The affected person has at least three or more of the following:</p>
<ul>
<li>Restlessness or feeling keyed up</li>
<li>Being easily fatigued</li>
<li>Difficulty concentrating or mind going blank</li>
<li>Irritability</li>
<li>Muscle tension</li>
<li>Sleep disturbance.</li>
</ul>
<p>In children just one symptom.</p>
<p>Most common in adults and female.</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="panic-disorder">Panic disorder<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#panic-disorder" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Recurrent unexpected panic attacks.</li>
<li>A panic attack is an abrupt surge of intense fear or intense discomfort that reaches a peak within minutes, and during which time four (or more) of the following symptoms occur:</li>
<li> Palpitations, pounding heart, accelerated heart rate</li>
<li> Sweating</li>
<li> Trembling or shaking</li>
</ul>
<p> Chest pain or discomfort
 Nausea or abdominal distress.
 Feeling dizzy, unsteady, lightheaded, or faint
 Derealization or depersonalization
 Fear of losing control or going crazy
 Paresthesia (numbness or tingling sensation)
 Sensation of shortness of breath or smothering
 Fear of dying
 Chills or hot flushes
 Feeling of chocking</p>
<p><img src="assets/images/image-20251228-5b07a23d.jpeg" alt="img-26.jpeg"></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p>At least one of the attacks has been followed by 1 month or more of either :</p>
</li>
<li>
<p> Persistent concern or worry about additional panic attacks or their consequences or</p>
</li>
<li>
<p> A significant maladaptive change in behavior related to the attacks</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Not attributed to substance effect, medical condition or another mental disorder.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="separation-anxiety-disorder">Separation Anxiety Disorder<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#separation-anxiety-disorder" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>
<p>Essential feature is excessive fear or anxiety concerning separation from home or attachment figures exceeding what may be expected at the given developmental level.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Individuals with separation anxiety disorder have symptoms that meet at least three of the following criteria: they experience persistent excessive fear when;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>separation from home or major attachment figures</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>worry about the well-being or death of attachment figures</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>worry about untoward events to themselves</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>reluctance or refusal to go out by themselves or being alone</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>reluctance or refusal to go to sleep alone</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>repeated nightmares</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Physiological features such as headache upon separation</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>The disturbance must last for a period of at least 4 weeks in children and adolescents and 6 months or more in adults</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>It causes significant distress or impairment in social, academic and occupational life.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Risk factors include: after life stress, parental overprotection and intrusiveness.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>The most prevalent anxiety disorder in children under 12yrs.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="selective-mutism">Selective Mutism<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#selective-mutism" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>
<p>Consistent failure to speak in specific social situations in which there is an expectation for speaking (e.g., at school) despite speaking in other situations for at least 1 month.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Such children do not initiate speech or reciprocally respond when spoken to by others except the very close family members or friends.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>It interferes with educational or occupational achievement or with social communication.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>The failure to speak is not attributable to a lack of knowledge of, or comfort with, the spoken language required in the social situation.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>The disturbance is not better explained by a communication disorder</p>
</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="specific-phobia">Specific Phobia<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#specific-phobia" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Revolves around specific or single feared objects or situation that is not in fact objectively dangerous</li>
<li>There's active avoidance of the phobic objects or situations lasting for 6 or more months.</li>
<li>The fear and anxiety is out of proportion and is the immediate response to the object or situation.</li>
</ul>

<span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mo></mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\circ</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.4445em;"></span><span class="mord"></span></span></span></span></span>  Cynophobia  dogs
<span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mo></mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\circ</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.4445em;"></span><span class="mord"></span></span></span></span></span>  Entomophobia  insects
<span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mo></mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\circ</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.4445em;"></span><span class="mord"></span></span></span></span></span>  Pyrophobia  fire</p>
<p><span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mo></mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\circ</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.4445em;"></span><span class="mord"></span></span></span></span></span>  Gephyrophobia  bridge crossing
