Psychiatric illnesses<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#2-psychiatric-illnesses" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ul>
<li>Current s/s of psychiatric disorders esp. mood disorders</li>
<li>Substance use disorders, anxiety disorders and personality(borderline &amp; antisocial).</li>
<li>Previous psychiatric dx and treatments and prognosis</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="3-history">3. History<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#3-history" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Previous suicide attempts, aborted suicide attempts or other self harming behaviors</li>
<li>Previous or current medical Dx and Rx including surgeries/hospitalizations</li>
<li>Family Hx of suicide/attempts or mental illness including substance abuse</li>
</ul>
<ol start="4">
<li>Psychosocial situation</li>
</ol>
<ul>
<li>Acute psychosocial crises and chronic psychosocial stressors-losses, finances, family...</li>
<li>Employment status, living situation (whether or not having children in the home) &amp; presence or absence of external supports.</li>
<li>Family constellation and quality of family relationships</li>
<li>Cultural/religious beliefs about death and suicide</li>
<li>Individual strengths and vulnerability</li>
</ul>
<ol start="5">
<li>Coping skills</li>
</ol>
<ul>
<li>Personality traits</li>
<li>Past responses to stress</li>
<li>Capacity for reality testing</li>
<li>Ability to tolerate psychological pain and satisfy psychological needs</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="assessment-of-suicidal-risk">Assessment of suicidal risk<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#assessment-of-suicidal-risk" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Use of different scales which assess for potential risk factors to suicide among others.</li>
<li>SADCHILDREN SCALE</li>
<li>SAD PERSONS SCALE</li>
<li>IS PATH WARM?</li>
</ul>
<p>Sad persons(Patterson et al, 1983)
Adapted sad persons' scale(Juhnke,1996)</p>
<ul>
<li>S: Sex.</li>
<li>Male: female=4:1 but females attempt more</li>
<li>A: Age.</li>
<li>High in Youth 15-24, males&gt;75 &amp; females 45-54 yrs</li>
<li>D: Depression.</li>
<li>Depressed are 20x than general population due to hopelessness</li>
<li>P: Prior history.</li>
<li>Approx 80% of completed suicides are preceded by a prior attempt.</li>
<li>E: Ethanol abuse.</li>
<li>Alcohol and/or drug abuse increase risk</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="sad-persons-cont">SAD PERSONS CONT'<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#sad-persons-cont" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>R: Rational thinking loss.</li>
<li>Psychosis (I had a voice telling me to kill myself)</li>
<li>S: support system loss.</li>
<li>Loss of support e.g. lover, relative, parent etc increase risk</li>
<li>O: Organized plan.</li>
<li>Having a method in mind creates more risk</li>
<li>N: No significant other</li>
<li>See s above</li>
<li>S: Sickness.</li>
<li>Terminal illness e.g. AIDS, cancer etc=20x</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="scoring-system">Scoring system<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#scoring-system" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>1 point for each positive answer on the above</li>
<li>Score &amp; risk</li>
<li>0-2: no real problem keep watch</li>
<li>3-4: send home but check frequently</li>
<li>3-6: consider hospitalization</li>
<li>7-10: definitely hospitalize involuntarily or voluntarily</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="sadchildren-scale-adapted-from-di-vasto-west-cristy-1979">'SADCHILDREN SCALE' (adapted from Di Vasto, West &amp; Cristy 1979)<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#sadchildren-scale-adapted-from-di-vasto-west-cristy-1979" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>S: support systems</li>
<li>A: alcohol/assault</li>
<li>D: depression/delusion</li>
<li>C: communication/change in behavior</li>
<li>H: hostility/hallucinations/history</li>
<li>I: impulsiveness/illness</li>
<li>L: lethality</li>
<li>D: demography</li>
<li>R: reaction of the evaluator</li>
<li>E: events leading to suicide attempt</li>
<li>N: no hope.</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="is-path-warm">IS PATH WARM?<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#is-path-warm" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>
<p>Suicide Ideation:</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Does client report active suicidal ideation?</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Written about suicide/death?</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Client report desire to kill self?</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Desire to purchase a weapon e.g. gun?</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Intention to use car, gun etc to kill self?</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Substance abuse:</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Client Excessively use alcohol or substances?</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Purposelessness:</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Does s/he voice lack/loss of purpose in life?</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Little or no reason to continue living?</p>
</li>
</ul>
<p><img src="assets/images/image-20251228-768a56c0.jpeg" alt="img-49.jpeg"></p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="anger">Anger:<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#anger" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<p>Client express feelings of range or uncontrolled anger?</p>
<ul>
<li>Seek revenge against others thought to have wronged or faulted him/her?</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="trapped">Trapped:<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#trapped" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<p>Does client feel trapped?
Believe no way out of h/her current situation?
Believe death is preferable to a painful living?
Believe no other choice remaining in life?</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="hopelessness">Hopelessness:<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#hopelessness" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<p>Negative sense of self, others and future?
Future appears hopeless with little chance for positive change?</p>
<p><img src="assets/images/image-20251228-768a56c0.jpeg" alt="img-50.jpeg"></p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="withdrawing">Withdrawing:<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#withdrawing" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<p>Indicate a desire to withdraw from family, friends etc
Has s/he already began withdrawing?</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="anxiety">Anxiety:<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#anxiety" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Feel anxious, agitated or unable to sleep?</li>
<li>Report inability to relax?
Report sleeping all time?</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="recklessness">Recklessness:<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#recklessness" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Act recklessly or engage in risky activities?</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="mood-change">Mood change:<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#mood-change" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Report experiencing dramatic mood shifts or states.</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="specific-interventions">Specific interventions<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#specific-interventions" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Psychopharmacology, especially the SSRIs.</li>
<li>Psychotherapy/CBT/ECT</li>
<li>Substance abuse treatment; treatment of pain disorders</li>
<li>Treatment of medical disorders</li>
<li>Involvement in outside activities/avoid isolation  join outside groups, bereavement groups, organizations</li>
<li>etc</li>
</ul>
<p><img src="assets/images/image-20251228-321c1400.jpeg" alt="img-51.jpeg"></p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="nursing-management-of-suicidal-patients">Nursing Management of suicidal patients<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#nursing-management-of-suicidal-patients" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Include;</li>
<li>Assess the patients suicidal potential.</li>
<li>Observe the patient for 24 hours.</li>
<li>Make sure the windows and electrical bulbs should not be access to the patients.</li>
<li>Remove all the dangerous objects such as, glass container, ashtrays, matches, cigarettes, ties, string, razor, blades, scissors or metal pins.</li>
<li>Stay with the patient and meet the physical needs of the patient.</li>
</ul>
<p><img src="assets/images/image-20251228-70ca8965.jpeg" alt="img-52.jpeg"></p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="nursing-care-cont">Nursing care cont'<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#nursing-care-cont" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Check the patient at frequent, irregular intervals during the night and ascertains safety and whereabouts.</li>
<li>All psychotropic drugs should be kept locked.</li>
<li>Ensure that the patient swallows prescribed medication.</li>
<li>Observe, record and report any changes in the client mood, elation, withdrawal in all the shifts.</li>
<li>Promote adequate nutrition, hydration and elimination.</li>
<li>Promote an adequate rest, sleep and activity.</li>
</ul>
<p><img src="assets/images/image-20251228-321c1400.jpeg" alt="img-53.jpeg"></p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="nursing-care-cont">Nursing care cont'<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#nursing-care-cont" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Do not joke about death, make sensitive remark such as "Everybody really want to live".</li>
<li>Do not argue about the patient's feelings.</li>
<li>Help the patient to identify positive aspects about him or herself and life situation.</li>
<li>Give the patient support to interact with others clients or to attend activities.</li>
<li>Give family psychotherapy for maintains of good interpersonal communication with the patient.</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="summary">SUMMARY<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#summary" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>
<p>NOTES:</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>END</p>
</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="violence-and-agression">VIOLENCE AND AGRESSION<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#violence-and-agression" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<p><img src="assets/images/image-20251228-14031833.jpeg" alt="img-54.jpeg"></p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="introduction">Introduction<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#introduction" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Violence and aggression are common psychiatric emergencies</li>
<li>Many psychiatric patients are not always violent or aggressive but these behaviors do occur during acute phases of psychiatric illnesses.</li>
<li>Health professionals should be well equipped with knowledge and skills to handle violent and/or aggressive patients.</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="causes">Causes<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#causes" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Organic and non-organic psychiatric conditions</li>
<li>Mania</li>
<li>Depression</li>
<li>Drug and alcohol dependence</li>
<li>Epilepsy</li>
<li>Acute stress reaction</li>
<li>Neurotic disorders</li>
<li>Impulsive violent behavior</li>
<li>Reactive psychosis</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="assessing-and-predicting-violent-behavior">Assessing and predicting violent behavior<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#assessing-and-predicting-violent-behavior" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Signs of impending violence:-</li>
<li>Very recent acts of violence including damage to property</li>
<li>Verbal or physical threats(menacing)</li>
<li>Carrying weapons that may be used to cause harm</li>
<li>Progressive psychomotor agitation</li>
<li>Alcohol or drug intoxication</li>
<li>Paranoid features in a psychotic patient</li>
<li>Command violent auditory hallucinations</li>
</ul>
<p><img src="assets/images/image-20251228-321c1400.jpeg" alt="img-55.jpeg"></p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="f69cca79">Cont<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#f69cca79" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ul>
<li>Catatonic excitement</li>
<li>Certain patients with mania</li>
<li>Certain patients with agitated depression</li>
<li>etc</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="assessing-the-risk-of-violence">Assessing the risk of violence<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#assessing-the-risk-of-violence" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Considerations:</li>
<li>Violent ideations and plans: idea, wish, intention, plan, availability of means, implementation of plan and wish for help.</li>
<li>Demographics: sex (males), age (15-24), socioeconomic status (low), social supports (few/absent).</li>
<li>Past history: violence, non-violent antisocial acts, impulse dyscontrol e.g. Gambling, substance use etc</li>
<li>Overt stressors: marital conflicts, losses-real or symbolic weaknesses etc</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="management">Management.<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#management" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>4 progressive strategies:-</li>
<li>De-escalation(defusing/talking down)</li>
<li>Environmental manipulation</li>
<li>Rapid tranquilization</li>
<li>Restrains and seclusion</li>
</ul>
<p><img src="assets/images/image-20251228-1ab28383.jpeg" alt="img-56.jpeg"></p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="common-drugs-used-for-rapid-tranquillization">Common drugs used for rapid tranquillization<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#common-drugs-used-for-rapid-tranquillization" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>A mixture of benzodiazepines with antipsychotics offer the best results.</li>
<li>Diazepam: 5-10 mg po/iv, max 30mg/event</li>
<li>Lorazepam: 2mg iv, max 10mg/24hrs</li>
<li>Olanzepine: 5-10mg im, max 30mg/event</li>
<li>Haloperidol: 5-10mg im, max 20mg/event</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="precautions-to-take">Precautions to take<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#precautions-to-take" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Speak with the patient in a calm voice</li>
<li>Do not argue with them</li>
<li>Approach them in an open posture</li>
<li>Always approach the from the side</li>
<li>Call them by their names</li>
<li>Do not put on dangling attires like scuffs, ties, necklaces etc</li>
<li>Remove any dangerous item that they may use to cause harm</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="what-to-do-in-case-of-attempted-attacks">What to do in case of attempted attacks<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#what-to-do-in-case-of-attempted-attacks" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Hold their hands from behind</li>
<li>Throw a heavy cloth e.g. blanket on the patient then restrain</li>
<li>Call for help (ensure enough staff back-up)</li>
<li>Make use of exit points</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="guidelines-for-self-protection-when-handling-an-aggressive-patients">Guidelines for self protection when handling an aggressive patients<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#guidelines-for-self-protection-when-handling-an-aggressive-patients" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Be prepared to move, a violent patient can strike out suddenly.</li>
<li>Keep comfortable distance away from the patient</li>
<li>Never see a potentially violent patient alone</li>
<li>Maintain a clear exit route for both the staff and patient</li>
<li>Be sure the patient has no weapons in his/her possessions</li>
<li>Administer prescribed anti-psychotic medications</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="catatonic-stupor">CATATONIC STUPOR<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#catatonic-stupor" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Stupor is a clinical syndrome of akinesia and mutism with preservation of consciousness.</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="management">MANAGEMENT<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#management" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ul>
<li>Ensure patent airway</li>
<li>Administer IV fluids</li>
<li>Collect hx and perform physical examinations</li>
<li>Draw blood for investigations before starting any treatment</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="case-scenario">Case scenario.<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#case-scenario" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>
<p>You are alone in the psychiatric nursing station doing documentations while your two colleagues are outside attending to patients. All of a sudden, Kamwenja, a manic patient known to exhibit violent behavior enters the room holding a dart on his right hand, he closes the door behind him and smilingly tells you; your day has finally come! Kwisha!</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Quiz: what will you do?</p>
</li>
</ul>
<p><img src="assets/images/image-20251228-70ca8965.jpeg" alt="img-57.jpeg"></p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="end">END<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#end" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>QUESTIONS?</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="therapies-in-mental-health">THERAPIES IN MENTAL HEALTH<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#therapies-in-mental-health" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<p>M. M. Z</p>
<p>12/28/2025</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="objectives">Objectives<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#objectives" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<p>By the end of the lesson, learners should be able to:</p>
<ul>
<li>Describe and apply the therapeutic nurse-client relationship.</li>
<li>Describe the various therapies including cognitive behavioral, social support, occupational, group, environmental, community based rehabilitation and electroconvulsive therapies.</li>
<li>Review pharmacological therapy.</li>
</ul>
<p>12/28/2025</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="therapeutic-nurse-client-relationship">THERAPEUTIC NURSE-CLIENT RELATIONSHIP<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#therapeutic-nurse-client-relationship" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>
<p>Therapeutic relationships are goal-oriented and directed at learning and growth promotion.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Such require:</p>
</li>
<li>
<p> Rapport, Self understanding, Acceptance, Consistency, Trust, Genuineness, Respect, Empathy</p>
</li>
</ul>
<p>12/28/2025</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="phases-of-a-therapeutic-nurse-client-relationship">Phases of a Therapeutic Nurse-Client Relationship<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#phases-of-a-therapeutic-nurse-client-relationship" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li> Pre-interaction phase</li>
<li> Orientation/Introductory Period</li>
<li> Working</li>
<li> Termination</li>
</ul>
<p>12/28/2025</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="psychotherapy">PSYCHOTHERAPY<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#psychotherapy" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Psychotherapy includes treatments of emotional, behavioral, personality and psychotic disorders based primarily on verbal and non-verbal communication with patients and their environmental, occupational and community support based needs.</li>
<li>Recovery of mentally ill patients is not dependent on biological treatment alone!</li>
</ul>
<p>12/28/2025</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="milieu-therapy">MILIEU THERAPY<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#milieu-therapy" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Also referred to as therapeutic environment or therapeutic community.</li>
<li>The environment is structured to effect behavioral changes and improve psychological health and functioning of the individual.</li>
</ul>
<p>12/28/2025</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="conditions-promoting-a-therapeutic-environment">Conditions Promoting a Therapeutic Environment<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#conditions-promoting-a-therapeutic-environment" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Basic physiological needs should be met.</li>
<li>Physical facilities are conducive to achievement of therapy goals e.g. space</li>
<li>Participates in decision making and problem solving.</li>
<li>Responsibilities assigned according to client capabilities.</li>
<li>Structured program of social and work related activities.</li>
<li>Community and family are involved.</li>
</ul>
<p>12/28/2025</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="role-of-the-nurse">Role of the Nurse<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#role-of-the-nurse" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Ensures basic needs for the client are met</li>
<li>Assessing physical and psychosocial status</li>
<li>Administering medications</li>
<li>Helping clients develop trusting relationships</li>
<li>Setting limits on unacceptable behaviors</li>
<li>Educating clients</li>
</ul>
<p>12/28/2025</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="group-therapy">GROUP THERAPY<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#group-therapy" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Involves treatment of an individual within a group through support and encouragement for the group members and the therapist.</li>
<li>It is a learning and problem solving process in which each individual is involved with his own self and the group is involved as a collective self.</li>
</ul>
<p>12/28/2025</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="classification-of-groups">Classification of groups<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#classification-of-groups" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<p>There are a number of group classifications:</p>
<ul>
<li> Open and closed</li>
<li> Structured and non-structured</li>
<li> Heterogeneous and homogeneous</li>
</ul>
<p>The classification that is of significance is one that distinguishes groups according to the method used:</p>
<p>12/28/2025</p>
<ol>
<li>Didactic  inspirational groups</li>
</ol>
<p>Emphasizes the educational experiences of its members and promotes intellectual and emotional changes while reflecting ethical, religious or societal values.</p>
<p>Examples:</p>
<ul>
<li>Alcoholics anonymous</li>
<li>Sex/relationship education</li>
<li>Discharge planning</li>
<li>Diet group</li>
</ul>
<p>12/28/2025</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="2-conversation-exploratory">2. Conversation/exploratory<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#2-conversation-exploratory" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ul>
<li>Exploration and <strong>verbalization</strong> of its members emotional and psychological problems within the context of their past and present relationship and their interpersonal relationships in the group.</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>Examples:</strong></p>
<ul>
<li> Personal growth group</li>
<li> Family therapy</li>
<li> Psychodrama</li>
<li> Marriage therapy.</li>
</ul>
<p>12/28/2025</p>
<p>12/28/2025</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="3-activity-groups">3. Activity groups<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#3-activity-groups" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ul>
<li>Uses a particular activity as the structure around which the interaction of the group members is built, encouraging the development of ego strengths and control.</li>
</ul>
<p>Examples:</p>
<ul>
<li> Music therapy</li>
<li> Play therapy</li>
<li> Exercise group</li>
<li> Reality orientation</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="curative-factors-in-group-therapy">Curative factors in group therapy<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#curative-factors-in-group-therapy" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>
<p>Shared information:
Because of similar backgrounds and problems the group members get the opportunity to share very important information.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Altruism:
An opportunity to help members of the group who may feel worthless and useless boost their ego.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<p>12/28/2025</p>
<ul>
<li>
<p>Universality:</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Sharing of experiences and finding that others respond positively lead to the discovery that problems, feelings and behaviour are not unique but are shared by others.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Group cohesion:</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>A feeling of belonging and empathy develops and the group becomes an important source of support.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<p>12/28/2025</p>
<p>Hope:</p>
<ul>
<li>Observing how members progress and overcome their problems gives the other group members hope.</li>
<li>Confidence in therapeutic process is engendered and group members begin to have confidence that their conditions will improve.</li>
</ul>
<p>12/28/2025</p>
<ul>
<li>
<p>Interpersonal learning:</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Group members not only learning from others but also analyze their personal feelings and behaviour in the group.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Ventilation:</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>This encompasses active, verbal participation in the group process by means of self disclosure and self-examination and helps in the release of negative feelings.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<p>12/28/2025</p>
<ul>
<li>Socialization:</li>
<li>Group members learn new, socially acceptable behavioural pattern. They receive frank feedback in a supportive environment about an acceptable behaviour and are encouraged to try new patterns.</li>
</ul>
<p>12/28/2025</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="phases-of-group-development">Phases of Group Development<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#phases-of-group-development" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Objectives, selection of members, the type of group, consultation with members, logistics and establishment of roles.</li>
<li>II. Middle/working phase</li>
<li>problem solving and decision making phase.</li>
<li>III. Final/Termination phase</li>
<li>after the groups objectives have been met, then it has to be terminated as required.</li>
</ul>
<p>12/28/2025</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="tasks-of-group-therapist-during-the-sessions">Tasks of group therapist during the sessions<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#tasks-of-group-therapist-during-the-sessions" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="preparation">Preparation<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#preparation" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ul>
<li> Set the objectives of the sessions.</li>
<li> Selection of group members.</li>
<li> Selection of the type of the group.</li>
<li> Consultation with the team: logistics arrangements.</li>
<li> Preparation of the group members.</li>
</ul>
<p>12/28/2025</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="maintenance-and-goal-achievement">Maintenance and goal achievement<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#maintenance-and-goal-achievement" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<p>The group leader is responsible for the group survival and achievement of its objectives through:</p>
<ul>
<li>Creation of therapeutic group norms such as confidentiality, frank as possible about feelings</li>
<li>Creation of a focal point: help all the members focus in a well planned activity (in the case of activity group).</li>
</ul>
<p>12/28/2025</p>
<ul>
<li>Management of problem behavior: such as people who monopolizes the group, people who all talk at the same time, late arrivals, losing contact with reality or becoming aggressive.</li>
<li>Creation of group cohesion: show respect, warmth and empathy to all the members and teach all of them to do the same by example.</li>
</ul>
<p>12/28/2025</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="termination">Termination<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#termination" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<p> Members are usually very dependent on one another and resistant to termination.
 Feelings of anger, loss, and affection should be verbalized and members encouraged to evaluate the entire group experience.
 Group leader to allow enough time for this phase.</p>
<p>12/28/2025</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="occupational-therapy">OCCUPATIONAL THERAPY<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#occupational-therapy" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Treatment through active participation in purposeful activities</li>
<li>It also emphasizes development of ones' occupational interests, skills and abilities.</li>
<li>Aim:</li>
<li>To rehabilitate patients for their return home and help them overcome anxiety at work or deal with a difficult working relationship.</li>
</ul>
<p>12/28/2025</p>
<ul>
<li>Depending with the available resources various activities may be incorporated such as:</li>
<li> Gardening</li>
<li> Cooking/washing</li>
<li> Carpentry</li>
<li> Recreational activities e.g games</li>
<li> Intellectual activities: Group discussions, reading magazines</li>
</ul>
<p>12/28/2025</p>
<ul>
<li>The therapist role in this case involves:</li>
<li>Assessment</li>
<li>this helps in planning adequate occupational therapy programs</li>
<li>Rehabilitation</li>
<li>through the use of purposeful activities and attainment of satisfying personal relationships by encouraging new skills</li>
</ul>
<p>12/28/2025</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="cognitive-behavioral-therapy-cbt">COGNITIVE - BEHAVIORAL THERAPY (CBT)<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#cognitive-behavioral-therapy-cbt" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Involves changing one's attitudes and behavior by focusing on the automatic thoughts, images, beliefs and attitudes that are held and how these processes relate to the way a person behaves, as a way of dealing with emotional problems.</li>
</ul>
<p>12/28/2025</p>
<ul>
<li>The general goals in cognitive - behavioral therapy are:</li>
<li> To obtain symptom relief as quickly as possible,</li>
<li> to assist the client in identifying dysfunctional patterns of thinking and behaving,</li>
<li> to guide the client to evidence and logic that effectively tests the validity of the dysfunctional thinking.</li>
</ul>
<p>12/28/2025</p>
<ul>
<li>The client is asked to describe evidence that both supports and disputes the distorted thought. The logic underlying the inferences is then reviewed with the client.</li>
<li>Evaluation and discussion of the clients thoughts and the implication of their consequences.</li>
</ul>
<p>12/28/2025</p>
<ul>
<li>CBT can be used in the management of:</li>
<li>Anger, anxiety and panic attacks</li>
<li>Depression</li>
<li>Drug or substance abuse disorders</li>
<li>Eating disorders</li>
<li>Phobias</li>
<li>Obsessive  compulsive disorder</li>
<li>Child and adolescents problems</li>
<li>Post  traumatic stress disorders</li>
<li>Sexual and relationships problems etc.</li>
</ul>
<p>12/28/2025</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="electroconvulsive-therapy-ect">ELECTROCONVULSIVE THERAPY(ECT)<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#electroconvulsive-therapy-ect" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Induction of a grand mal seizure by means of an electrical pulse through the brain of an anaesthetized patient.</li>
<li>The mechanism of ECT is not clear, however it has been shown to affect neurotransmitters including GABA, norepinephrine, serotonin, dopamine and endogenous opiates.</li>
</ul>
<p>12/28/2025</p>
<p><img src="assets/images/image-20251228-67b7743e.jpeg" alt="img-58.jpeg"></p>
<p>12/28/2025</p>
<ul>
<li>It is given in doses ranging from 70 to 130 volts via electrodes placed on the temporal lobes.</li>
<li>The frequency of treatment depends upon the severity of the patient's mental disorder to a maximum of 8 to 12 sessions.</li>
</ul>
<p>12/28/2025</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="pre-treatment-evaluation">Pre-treatment Evaluation<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#pre-treatment-evaluation" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Informed consent</li>
<li>Medical history and physical examination</li>
<li>Investigations such as full haemogram, UECs, EEG, ECG, chest and spinal x-ray if possible</li>
<li>Pre-medications and NPO.</li>
</ul>
<p>12/28/2025</p>
<p>12/28/2025</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="indications-for-ect">Indications for ECT<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#indications-for-ect" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>All mood disorders</li>
<li>Major depressive episodes</li>
<li>Acute schizophrenic presentations</li>
<li>Catatonic excitement</li>
<li>its merely suggested in: delirium and several medical conditions such as parkinsons disease</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="contraindications">Contraindications<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#contraindications" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>There are no absolute contraindications; Relative contraindications include;</li>
<li> Increased intracranial pressure</li>
<li> Recent history of myocardial infarction</li>
<li> High-risk conditions e.g. bleeding (or otherwise unstable), vascular aneurysm or malformation, intracerebral haemorrhage, acute or impending retinal detachment, pheochromocytoma, or high anaesthetic risk</li>
</ul>
<p>12/28/2025</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="side-effects-of-ect">Side Effects of ECT<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#side-effects-of-ect" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Anxiety and apprehension</li>
<li>Confusion</li>
<li>Memory loss</li>
<li>Headaches, which respond to acetaminophen or NSAIDS</li>
<li>Transient muscle aches</li>
</ul>
<p>12/28/2025</p>
<p>Less Common Side Effects:</p>
<ul>
<li>Weight gain, possibly due to treatment of anorexia</li>
<li>Amenorrhea or other menstrual changes lasting up to several months</li>
<li>Transient systemic hypertension</li>
<li>Apnea or laryngospasms</li>
<li>Burns from poor contact with electrodes</li>
<li>Cardiac arrhythmias</li>
<li>Prolonged (usually defined as &gt;3 minutes) seizure or a "late" seizure</li>
</ul>
<p>12/28/2025</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="nursing-care-in-ect">Nursing Care in ECT<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#nursing-care-in-ect" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Electroconvulsive therapy is treated like a minor surgical procedure that requires preoperative and postoperative care:</li>
<li> Providing educational and emotional support</li>
<li> Pre-treatment planning and assessment</li>
<li> Preparing and monitoring the patient during the actual procedure</li>
<li> Post-treatment care and evaluation</li>
</ul>
<p>12/28/2025</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="providing-educational-and-emotional-support">Providing Educational and emotional support<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#providing-educational-and-emotional-support" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Explain the procedure to the patient</li>
<li>Obtain an informed consent from the patient and the guardian.</li>
<li>Respond to patient's concerns and feelings.</li>
<li>Educate the patient concerning the procedure and explain to the patient the necessary tasks associated with ECT.</li>
</ul>
<p>12/28/2025</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="pre-treatment-nursing-care">Pre-treatment Nursing care<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#pre-treatment-nursing-care" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Preparation of treatment room for the ECT procedure</li>
<li>Complete the pre-treatment check list.</li>
<li>Patient's identity is checked and the patient wears an identity bracelet.</li>
<li>Safekeeping of the patient's valuables.</li>
<li>NPO for minimum 4 hours before treatment.</li>
<li>The patient's hair should be clean and dry to allow for electrode contact.</li>
</ul>
<p>12/28/2025</p>
<ul>
<li>Empty bladder before treatment.</li>
<li>Prostheses, dentures, glasses, hearing aids, contact lenses should be removed.</li>
<li>Minimise anxiety through anxiety management techniques, ensuring short waiting time and offering reassurance and support.</li>
<li>Standard practices should be practiced regarding general anaesthesia care</li>
</ul>
<p>12/28/2025</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="nursing-care-during-ect-procedure">Nursing Care during ECT Procedure<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#nursing-care-during-ect-procedure" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Patient in a well padded bed and placed in a comfortable dorsal position or supine position. A small pillow is placed under the lumber curve.</li>
<li>Apply ECG electrodes, BP cuff, and pulse oximetry sensor.</li>
<li>Give a short acting anesthetic agent.</li>
</ul>
<p>12/28/2025</p>
<ul>
<li>Support the shoulder and arms of the patient. Restraint the thigh with the help of a sheet.</li>
<li>Hyperextension of the head with support to the chin.</li>
<li>Administer oxygen</li>
<li>Apply jelly to the electrodes</li>
<li>Make the observations of the convulsions, suction and <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi mathvariant="normal">O</mi><mn>2</mn></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathrm{O}_2</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.8333em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathrm">O</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3011em;"><span style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">2</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s"></span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> if necessary.</li>
</ul>
<p>12/28/2025</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="post-ect-care">Post-ECT Care<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#post-ect-care" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Observe and record the vital parameters  hourly until stable</li>
<li>Place the patient on side lying position, clean the secretions</li>
<li>Allow the patient to sleep for 30 min to one hour</li>
<li>Reassure the client and reorient to the ward</li>
<li>Allow the patient to have tea or any drinks</li>
<li>Record the procedure</li>
</ul>
<p>12/28/2025</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="any-question">Any Question???<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#any-question" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<p><img src="assets/images/image-20251228-1f16011d.jpeg" alt="img-59.jpeg"></p>
<p>12/28/2025</p>
<ul>
<li>REVIEW PHARMACOLOGICAL THERAPY FOR MENTAL DISORDERS.</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="pharmacotherapy">PHARMACOTHERAPY<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#pharmacotherapy" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<p>Psychotropic drugs can be classified according to their uses:</p>
<ul>
<li> Antidepressants</li>
<li> Mood stabilizers</li>
<li> Antipsychotics</li>
<li> Anxiolytics and Hypnotics</li>
<li> Anticonvulsants</li>
<li> Psychostimulants.</li>
</ul>
<p>12/28/2025</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="anti-depressants">Anti Depressants<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#anti-depressants" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Antidepressant medication should always be tailored to the needs of individual patients titrating the dose against the clinical effect and side effect profile.</li>
<li>Treatment be introduced at the lowest dose possible and gradually increasing so as to reduce the severity of the initial side effects.</li>
<li>About 5 -10% of depression becomes chronic and requires regular follow up and continuous antidepressant medication.</li>
</ul>
<p>12/28/2025</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="classification-of-antidepressants">Classification of antidepressants<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#classification-of-antidepressants" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ol>
<li>Heterocyclics: block the uptake of noradrenalin or serotonin into presynaptic nerve terminals hence increasing their availability.</li>
</ol>
<ul>
<li>Bicyclics: Dothiepine</li>
<li>Tricyclics(TCA):</li>
<li>Amitriptyline (Tryptanol): 25-150mg/24hrs.</li>
<li>Others include: Maproptiline, Nortryptyline, Desipramine and Lofepramine, Trimipramine, Imipramine, Clomipramine</li>
<li>Tetracyclics:</li>
<li>Mianserine (Lantanon): 10-60mg/24hrs (nocte, start slow and increase slowly).</li>
</ul>
<p>12/28/2025</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="side-effects-of-heterocyclics">Side effects of heterocyclics<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#side-effects-of-heterocyclics" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Lethality in overdose except in mianserin, doses of over 1g can result in death, due to seizures, arrhythmias or hypotension.</li>
<li>Sedation</li>
<li>Anticholinergic side effects such as:</li>
<li> Blurred vision</li>
<li> Dry mouth</li>
<li> Urinary hesitancy and retention.</li>
<li> Tachycardia</li>
<li> Aggravation of glaucoma and constipation</li>
</ul>
<p>12/28/2025</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="cont-d">Cont'd...<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#cont-d" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Seizures e.g. with clomipramine.</li>
<li>Cardiovascular: Hypotension and orthostatic hypotension (alpha 1 receptor blockage).</li>
<li>Hematological: Leucopenia</li>
<li>Sexual: Decreased libido, Orgasmic dysfunction in females, delayed or occasional absence of ejaculation in males.</li>
<li>Weight gain resulting from an increased appetite</li>
<li>Depersonalization/ derealization.</li>
<li>Use in the first trimester of pregnancy should be avoided. Excreted into breast milk.</li>
</ul>
<p>12/28/2025</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="contraindications">Contraindications<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#contraindications" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Acute myocardial infarction</li>
<li>Pregnancy</li>
<li>Breast feeding</li>
<li>Alcoholism</li>
<li>Glaucoma</li>
<li>Epilepsy</li>
</ul>
<p>12/28/2025</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="2-selective-serotonin-re-uptake-inhibitors-ssris">2. Selective Serotonin Re-uptake Inhibitors (SSRIs)<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#2-selective-serotonin-re-uptake-inhibitors-ssris" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ul>
<li>Selectively inhibits serotonin reuptake, alleviating depression and imparting some anti-anxiety effect.</li>
<li>Has got fewer side effects than Tricyclics.</li>
</ul>
<p>Examples:</p>
<ul>
<li>Fluoxetine (prozac):  20-80mg/24hrs</li>
<li>Paroxetine (aropax):  20-80mg/24hrs</li>
<li>Others: citalopram, fluvoxamine, sertraline.</li>
</ul>
<p>12/28/2025</p>
<p>12/28/2025</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="cont-d">Cont'd...<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#cont-d" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Side effects of SSRIs:</li>
<li>Nausea and vomiting, Diarrhea</li>
<li>Tremors, Restlessness</li>
<li>Dizziness, headache, Insomnia</li>
<li>Excessive sweating</li>
<li>Ejaculation delay and reduced libido</li>
<li>Suppression of cytochrome p450 just like the tricyclics thus increasing the blood concentration of antipsychotic and other antidepressants if combined.</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="monoamine-oxidase-inhibitors-maois">Monoamine oxidase inhibitors (MAOIs)<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#monoamine-oxidase-inhibitors-maois" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>These drugs act by inhibiting the MAO enzyme, thereby causing an increase in biogenic amines such as noradrenaline, dopamine and serotonin in the storage sites throughout the central nervous system.</li>
<li>Phenelzine (Nardil).</li>
<li>Tranylcypromine (Parnate).</li>
<li>Precautions: Pregnancy, Peadiatrics, Breastfeeding and Geriatrics</li>
</ul>
<p>12/28/2025</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="side-effects-of-maois">Side effects of MAOIs<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#side-effects-of-maois" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Dizziness, tiredness and weakness</li>
<li>Diarrhoea</li>
<li>Swelling of the feet and lower limbs</li>
<li>Unusual excitement or nervousness</li>
<li>Tachycardia</li>
<li>Dark urine, difficulty urinating,</li>
<li>Headaches</li>
<li>Skin rash</li>
<li>Blurred vision, constipation</li>
<li>Decreased libido</li>
<li>Difficulty sleeping.</li>
</ul>
<p>12/28/2025</p>
