<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="contraindications">Contraindications<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#contraindications" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Cardiovascular disease</li>
<li>Severe liver and renal functioning impairment</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="patient-information">Patient information<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#patient-information" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Morning administration to avoid sleep disturbance</li>
<li>Food and beverages containing Tyramine to be avoided during treatment or 14 days after completion of treatment:</li>
<li>Alcohol (beer and chianti wine), avocado, broad beans, chocolate, cream and yoghurt, meat or fish preserved through smoking or pickling, yeast products, cheese.</li>
</ul>
<p>12/28/2025</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="factors-influencing-the-choice-of-antidepressants">Factors influencing the choice of antidepressants<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#factors-influencing-the-choice-of-antidepressants" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Previous response</li>
<li>Family history of response</li>
<li>Agitation or retardation</li>
<li>Cost.</li>
<li>Co-morbid disorders.</li>
<li>History of cardiac disease (avoid heterocyclics, except for mianserine).</li>
<li>Epilepsy (avoid heterocyclics particularly clomipramine and maprotiline).</li>
<li>Glaucoma (avoid heterocyclics which are more anticholinergics).</li>
</ul>
<p>12/28/2025</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="mood-stabilizers">Mood Stabilizers<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#mood-stabilizers" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="lithium-carbonate">Lithium carbonate<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#lithium-carbonate" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h3 level="3" id="indications">Indications:<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#indications" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h3></div>
<ul>
<li>Bipolar mood disorder: acute phase of mania for maintenance or prophylaxis.</li>
<li>Cyclothymic disorder</li>
<li>Schizoaffective disorder: bipolar type.</li>
<li>Other uses: psychosis due to tricyclis, organic brain syndrome, aggression, postpartum mania.</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h3 level="3" id="treatment-principles">Treatment principles:<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#treatment-principles" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h3></div>
<ul>
<li>Prior to the beginning of treatment, inform the patient about:</li>
<li>Side effects and dangers</li>
<li>The possibilities that diuretics and anti-inflammatory drugs may increase lithium serum levels to dangerous limits.</li>
<li>Avoiding alteration in sodium intake and dehydration.</li>
</ul>
<p>12/28/2025</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="pharmacokinetics">Pharmacokinetics<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#pharmacokinetics" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Lithium taken by mouth is well absorbed from the intestine.</li>
<li>It is not bound to plasma.</li>
<li>Lithium absorption is linked to Na balance in the body; lithium decrease sodium re-absorption in the proximal and distal convoluted tubules causing natriuresis and sub-clinical sodium depletion.</li>
<li>If Na intake is lowered or loss increased (diuretics, diarrhea, sweating) there is an increased tubular uptake of lithium in place of Na with an added risk of toxicity.</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="mechanism-of-action">Mechanism of action<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#mechanism-of-action" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Lithium inhibits presynaptic alpha and post synaptic beta adrenergic mechanisms. It replaces intracellular Na and by doing so decreases cellular excitability.</li>
</ul>
<p>12/28/2025</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="patient-monitoring">Patient monitoring<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#patient-monitoring" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ol>
<li>Before starting lithium</li>
</ol>
<ul>
<li>Complete medical hx and physical examination</li>
<li>Laboratory determination of:</li>
<li>Full blood count</li>
<li>Urea and electrolytes</li>
<li>Thyroid function tests</li>
<li>Electrocardiogram (those with hx of heart disease)</li>
</ul>
<ol start="2">
<li>After starting lithium</li>
</ol>
<ul>
<li>Coz of narrow therapeutic and toxic levels, do regular lithium serum levels (0.6  1.2mmol/liter). Dosages are therefore based on the lithium serum levels.</li>
</ul>
<ol start="3">
<li>Administration of the medicine</li>
</ol>
<ul>
<li>With food to avoid gastric irritation</li>
<li>Drink plenty of fluids in hot weather or when exercising.</li>
<li>Diet to contain enough Na+ otherwise toxic symptoms develop on lower dosages of lithium.</li>
<li>If a dose is missed, take as soon as possible unless it is within six hours of the next scheduled dose. Do not increase the next dose.</li>
</ul>
<p>12/28/2025</p>
<ol start="4">
<li>Side effects</li>
</ol>
<p>Side effects of lithium are increased if a person is dehydrated; if side effects occur try giving the person one or two glasses of water. Carbonated soft drinks are high in caffeine and may worsen the side effects.</p>
<p>Common side effects</p>
<ul>
<li>Weight gain</li>
<li>Stomach ache</li>
<li>Diarrhoea</li>
<li>Nausea</li>
<li>Vomiting</li>
<li>Increased thirst</li>
<li>Increase micturation</li>
<li>Fine hand tremor</li>
<li>Tiredness, weakness, dizziness and headache.</li>
</ul>
<p>12/28/2025</p>
<p>12/28/2025</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="occasional-side-effects">Occasional side effects<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#occasional-side-effects" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Low thyroid functioning or goitre</li>
<li>Acne</li>
<li>Skin rashes</li>
<li>Hair loss</li>
<li>Change in blood sugar</li>
<li>Metallic taste in the mouth</li>
<li>Irritability</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="uncommon-but-potentially-serious-side-effects-stop-the-lithium-and-inform-the-psychiatrist">Uncommon but potentially serious side effects (stop the lithium and inform the psychiatrist)<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#uncommon-but-potentially-serious-side-effects-stop-the-lithium-and-inform-the-psychiatrist" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Seizures</li>
<li>Confusion</li>
</ul>
<p>12/28/2025</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="signs-that-the-lithium-level-may-be-too-high">Signs that the lithium level may be too high<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#signs-that-the-lithium-level-may-be-too-high" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<p>(inform the psychiatrist immediately and do not give lithium for at least 24hrs)</p>
<ul>
<li>Vomiting or dirrhoea more than once</li>
<li>Sever trembling</li>
<li>Weakness</li>
<li>Lack of coordination</li>
<li>Extreme sleepiness or tiredness</li>
<li>Severe dizziness</li>
<li>Trouble speaking or slurred speech</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="serious-toxic-side-effects-admit-to-general-hospital-immediately">Serious toxic side effects (admit to general hospital immediately)<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#serious-toxic-side-effects-admit-to-general-hospital-immediately" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Irregular heart beat</li>
<li>Fainting</li>
<li>Staggering</li>
<li>Blurred vision</li>
<li>Ringing or buzzing sound in the ears</li>
<li>No urination</li>
<li>Muscle twitches, high fever, convulsions, unconsciousness</li>
</ul>
<ol start="5">
<li>Precautions</li>
</ol>
<ul>
<li>Some drugs increase lithium levels e.g. indocid and thiazide diuretics.</li>
<li>Do not take more than the prescribed dose</li>
<li>Do not drink large amounts of coffee, tea or carbonated drinks because of their diuretic effects</li>
<li>Lithium should never be taken during pregnancy because it can cause birth defects.</li>
</ul>
<p>12/28/2025</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="carbamazepine-tegretol">Carbamazepine (Tegretol).<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#carbamazepine-tegretol" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Is an anticonvulsant used to treat complex  partial and tonic clonic seizures. It has a mild mood stabilizing effect of patients.</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="indications-of-use">Indications of use:<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#indications-of-use" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ul>
<li>Bipolar disorder: acute mania. Effective in lithium - resistant bipolar disorder.</li>
<li>Affective symptoms secondary to seizure disorders</li>
<li>Impusive control problems: aggression,</li>
<li>Schizoaffective disorder.</li>
<li>Schizophrenia (not as a first line treatment).</li>
<li>Alcohol withdrawal (not as a first line treatment).</li>
</ul>
<p>12/28/2025</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="dosage-of-carbamazepine">Dosage of carbamazepine<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#dosage-of-carbamazepine" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Start with low dose (e.g. 100mg bd). The average therapeutic dose is 200mg tds but can be higher depending on clinical response and side effects.</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="side-effects-of-carbamazepine">Side effects of carbamazepine<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#side-effects-of-carbamazepine" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ul>
<li>Most common: sedation, vertigo, blurred vision, ataxia</li>
<li>Nausea, vomiting, slowing of cardiac conduction, rash may occur.</li>
<li>Serious side effects such as hepatitis, exfoliative dermatitis (steven-johnsons syndrome) and blood dyscrasias are extremely rare.</li>
</ul>
<p>12/28/2025</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="antipsychotics">ANTIPSYCHOTICS<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#antipsychotics" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="introduction">Introduction<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#introduction" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ul>
<li><strong>Antipsychotic drugs</strong> are also called major tranquilizers or neuroleptics used in the treatment of psychoses like schizophrenia, bipolar disorders (manic phase) and alcohol withdrawal disorder.</li>
</ul>
<table><thead><tr><th>GENERIC NAME</th><th>TRADE NAME</th><th>DAILY DOSES(RANGE)</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td><strong>Low Potency Drugs</strong></td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr><td>Chlorpromazine</td><td>Largactil</td><td>300-1000mgs</td></tr><tr><td>Sulpride</td><td>Domatil,Sulparex</td><td>200-2400mg</td></tr><tr><td>Thioridazine</td><td>Melleril</td><td>50-800mg</td></tr><tr><td><strong>High Potency Drugs</strong></td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr><td>Haloperidol</td><td>Haldol,Serenace</td><td>1-20mg</td></tr><tr><td>Thiothixene</td><td>Navane</td><td>6-60mgs</td></tr><tr><td>Zoxapine</td><td>Loxitane</td><td>60-250mgs</td></tr><tr><td>Molindone</td><td>Lidone</td><td>50-400mgs</td></tr><tr><td>Flupenthixol</td><td>Depixol</td><td>6-18mg</td></tr><tr><td>Fluphenazine</td><td>Moditen</td><td>2.5-20mg</td></tr></tbody></table>

<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="mechanisms-of-action">Mechanisms of Action<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#mechanisms-of-action" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>The drugs are thought to work by blocking dopamine receptors causing a decrease in psychotic symptoms.</li>
<li>metabolised in the liver and excreted by the kidneys. For one to get the desired effects, one must maintain the patient on the lowest dose possible and initial therapy should be on divided doses so that the patient can be monitored.</li>
</ul>
<p>For acutely psychotic patients:</p>
<ul>
<li>
<p>Give intramuscular haloperidol, for example, 5mg every 30 to 60 minutes over a two to six hour period. Peak level is attained 20 to 40 minutes after injection.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Monitor blood pressure before each dose and withhold if the systolic blood pressure is 90mm Hg or below.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Sleep state should be monitored to ensure six to seven hours of sleep.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Dystonia occurring 1 hour to 48 hours after starting treatment should be treated with an antiparkinsonism drug.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>To decrease the danger to the patient themselves and others, the patient needs to be monitored for possible adverse reactions to the medication.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Drugs should be given using the following time frame:</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Six months for first psychotic episode.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>One year period for second psychotic episode.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Indefinite period for third and later psychotic episodes.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>The drug should be discontinued through tapering the dosage to avoid dyskinesia.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="side-effects-of-antipsychotics">Side effects of antipsychotics<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#side-effects-of-antipsychotics" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>
<p>There are several side effects that may be experienced by patients. These include drowsiness and orthostatic hypotension, especially after im injections.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>The patient may also experience <strong>extra pyramidal symptoms</strong> like:</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Dystonia, that is, spasms of muscles of face, neck, back, eye, arms and legs.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Oculogyric crisis, presenting as fixed upward gaze from spasm of oculomotor muscles.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Torticollis, that is, pulling of the head to the side from spasm of cervical muscles.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="extrapyramidal-side-effects-of-antipsychotics-cntd">Extrapyramidal side effects of antipsychotics cntd...<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#extrapyramidal-side-effects-of-antipsychotics-cntd" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Opisthotonus, which refers to the hyperextension of the back from spasm of back muscles.</li>
<li>Akathisia or continuous motor restlessness.</li>
<li>Akinesia or lack of body movement especially arms.</li>
<li>Pseudoparkinsonism, which presents with a shuffling gait, mask-like facial expression, tremor, rigidity</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="side-effects-cntd">SIDE EFFECTS CNTD...<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#side-effects-cntd" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>The patient may also experience tardive dyskinesia, that is, a wormlike movement of the tongue, frequent blinking, and involuntary movement of tongue, lips and jaw. They may experience convulsive seizures or allergic or toxic effects (some of which are rare and serious). These include:</li>
<li>Aggranulosis</li>
<li>Oral monoliasis</li>
<li>Dermatitis</li>
<li>Jaundice</li>
</ul>
<p>Side effects of antipsychotics cntd</p>
<p> The patient may also exhibit other side effects including endocrine or metabolic effects like weight gain or decreased libido, impotence, impaired ejaculation in males. They may also have decreased thermoregulatory ability and as a result might complain of being too cold or too hot.</p>
<p> Adjusting the dosage of antipsychotic drugs, and giving antiparkinsonian drugs can often be quite effective in treating side</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="contraindications">Contraindications<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#contraindications" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Comatose, glaucoma, prosthetic hyperplastic, acute myocardial infarction are contraindications to the use of these drugs</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="d680b31f">Nurses Responsibility for a Patient Receiving Antipsychotics<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#d680b31f" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>
<p>Instruct the patient to take sips of water frequently to relieve dryness of mouth. Frequent mouth washes, use of chewing gum and applying glycerine.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>A high-fiber diet, increased fluid intake and laxatives if needed, help to reduce constipation.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Advise the patient to get up from the bed or chair very slowly. Patient should sit on the edge of the bed for one full minute dangling his feet, before standing up.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Check BP before and after medication is given as a measure to prevent falls and other complications resulting from orthostatic hypotension.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Differentiate between akathisia and agitation. A change of drug may be necessary if side-effects are severe.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Administer antiparkinsonian drugs as prescribed.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Observe the patient regularly for abnormal movements.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Take all seizure precautions.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Patient should be warned about driving a car or operating machinery when first treated with antipsychotics.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Giving the entire dose at bedtime usually eliminates any problem from sedation.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Advise the patient to use sunscreen measures (use of full sleeves, dark glasses etc) for photosensitive reactions.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Teach the importance of drug compliance, side-effects of drugs and reporting if too severe, regular follow-ups.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="anxiolytics-and-hypnotics">Anxiolytics and hypnotics<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#anxiolytics-and-hypnotics" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>The distinction between anxiolytics and hypnotics is artificial: most anxiolytics in higher doses given at night have sleep inducing actions and many hypnotics in divided doses during the day are useful anxiolytics.</li>
<li>Anxiolytics are those drugs whose main purpose is to decrease anxiety.</li>
<li>Hypnotic drugs have a calming effect, decrease arousal and promote sleep.</li>
<li>Hypnotics are often anxiolytics but not all anxiolytics have hypnotic properties.</li>
</ul>
<p>12/28/2025</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="classification">Classification<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#classification" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>There are many chemical groups of drugs that have sedative-hypnotic properties but just a few are used in modern psychiatry on a regular basis:</li>
<li>These are:</li>
<li> Benzodiazepines</li>
<li> Cyclopyrolones</li>
<li> Azapirones</li>
<li>Other less commonly used groups are: barbiturates, carbamates, cyclic esters, chloral hydrate and alcohol.</li>
<li>Antidepressants are often used in certain anxiety states as drugs of first choice.</li>
</ul>
<p>12/28/2025</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="anxiolytics-and-hypnotics">Anxiolytics and hypnotics<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#anxiolytics-and-hypnotics" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="mode-of-action">Mode of action<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#mode-of-action" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ul>
<li>Both benzodiazepines and cyclopyrones act primarily on GABA  benzodiazepine receptor complex facilitating the effect of GABA.</li>
<li>Buspirone the only available azapirone is a 5HT1A partial agonist and a non-sedating, non-hypnotic anxiolytic.</li>
<li>BDZ are powerful potentiators of GABA activity:</li>
<li>Muscle relaxation both pre and post synaptic influences in the spinal cord.</li>
<li>Anticonvulsant effects by general inhibiting effect</li>
<li>Ataxia by a cerebellar effect.</li>
<li>Sedation by the effects on the reticular activating system.</li>
</ul>
<p>12/28/2025</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="anxiolytics-and-hypnotics">Anxiolytics and hypnotics<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#anxiolytics-and-hypnotics" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<p>For clinical purposes, benzodiazepines and related compounds are classified as follows:</p>
<ul>
<li>Short acting (half life less than 24hrs).</li>
<li>Intermediate acting (half life between 24 and 48 hrs).</li>
<li>Long acting (half life more than 48 hrs).</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="anxiolytics">Anxiolytics<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#anxiolytics" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ul>
<li>Short acting e.g. diazepam (valium), od.</li>
<li>Intermediate acting e.g. clozabam (Urbanol) bd.</li>
<li>Long acting e.g Lorazepam (ativan) tds.</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="hypnotics">Hypnotics<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#hypnotics" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<p>Short acting, strongly sedative e.g. Temazepam (Normison)</p>
<p>12/28/2025</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="clinical-use-of-anxiolytics-and-hypnotics">CLINICAL USE OF ANXIOLYTICS AND HYPNOTICS<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#clinical-use-of-anxiolytics-and-hypnotics" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Treatment of choice in the management of anxiety, insomnia and stress.</li>
<li>Patients with fluctuating anxiety may prefer shorter acting oxazepam or lorazepam.</li>
<li>Alprozolam has been found to be useful in anxiety and depression.</li>
<li>Oxazepam penetrates BBB too slowly for a hypnotic effect, hence temazepam and lormetazepam are more appropriate.</li>
<li>BDZ are useful in the management of alcohol withdrawal syndrome: there is however a danger of substitution.</li>
<li>Diazepam has been used in the treatment of spasticity, tetanus and rabies.</li>
<li>Diazepam IV is used for status epilepticus.</li>
<li>Adverse effects of benzodiazepines are high potential for dependence and abuse.</li>
</ul>
<p>12/28/2025</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="anticonvusants-and-psychstimulants">Anticonvusants and psychstimulants<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#anticonvusants-and-psychstimulants" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Please study the following:</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="anticonvulsants">Anticonvulsants:<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#anticonvulsants" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ul>
<li>Phenytoin (hydantoin)</li>
<li>Carbamazepine</li>
<li>Barbiturates (phenobarbitone)</li>
<li>Succinamides (zarontin, celontin and milontin).</li>
<li>Benzodiazepines</li>
<li>Sodium valproate (epilim)</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="psychostimulants">Psychostimulants:<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#psychostimulants" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ul>
<li>Methylphenidate</li>
<li>Disulfiram</li>
</ul>
<p>12/28/2025</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="please-study-the-following">Please study the following:<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#please-study-the-following" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Agents used to treat extrapyramidal syndromes:</li>
<li> Anticholinergic drugs: biperiden, benzhexol, ophenadrine</li>
<li> Amantadine</li>
<li> Propranolol</li>
</ul>
<p>END</p>
<p>12/28/2025</p>
<p><img src="assets/images/image-20251228-e7ffc4f9.jpeg" alt="img-60.jpeg"></p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="community-mental-health">COMMUNITY MENTAL HEALTH<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#community-mental-health" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<p>BY M. M. Z</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="introduction">Introduction<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#introduction" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Community as a client</li>
<li>Populations in the community are at risk of many mental problems</li>
<li>Risks are associated with the crises they undergo in life</li>
<li>Both maturational and situational crises apply.</li>
</ul>
<p><img src="assets/images/image-20251228-e8df1b3b.jpeg" alt="img-61.jpeg"></p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="role-of-the-nurse-in-cmh">Role of the nurse in cmh<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#role-of-the-nurse-in-cmh" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li> Identification of mentally ill persons in the community</li>
<li> Provide first aid in psychiatric emergency care</li>
<li> Follow-up</li>
<li> Mental health education</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="public-health-model">Public health model<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#public-health-model" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Primary prevention</li>
<li>Secondary prevention</li>
<li>Tertiary prevention</li>
</ul>
<p><img src="assets/images/image-20251228-17180a3a.jpeg" alt="img-62.jpeg"></p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="primary-prevention">Primary prevention<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#primary-prevention" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Services aimed at reducing the incidence of mental disorders within the population.</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id=""><span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Focus on:-</li>
</ul>
<ol>
<li>Assisting individuals to increase their ability to cope effectively with stress.</li>
<li>Targeting and diminishing harmful forces (stressors) within the environment</li>
</ol>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="primary-interventions">Primary interventions<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#primary-interventions" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<p>Teaching:</p>
<ul>
<li>Parenting skills and child development to prospective new parents</li>
<li>Physical and psychosocial effects of alcohol/drugs</li>
<li>Techniques of stress management</li>
<li>Groups of individuals ways to cope with the changes associated with various maturational stages</li>
</ul>
<p>Cont:</p>
<ul>
<li>Teaching concepts of mental health to various groups within the community</li>
<li>Providing education and support to unemployed or homeless individuals</li>
<li>Providing education and support to other individuals in various transitional periods (e.g. widows and widowers, new retirees, and women entering the work force in middle life)</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="settings">Settings<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#settings" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Community social institutions e.g.:</li>
<li>Churches</li>
<li>Schools/colleges</li>
<li>Community centers</li>
<li>Workplaces</li>
<li>Meetings of women/youth groups</li>
<li>Civil society organizations</li>
<li>Etc</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="secondary-prevention">Secondary prevention<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#secondary-prevention" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Interventions aimed at minimizing early symptoms of psychiatric illness and directed toward reducing the prevalence and duration of the illness.</li>
</ul>
<p>6</p>
<ul>
<li>Focus:</li>
</ul>
<ol>
<li>Recognition of symptoms</li>
<li>Provision of treatment</li>
<li>Referral for treatment.</li>
</ol>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="secondary-interventions">Secondary interventions<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#secondary-interventions" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Ongoing assessment of individuals at high risk for illness exacerbation</li>
<li>Provision of care for individuals in whom illness symptoms have been assessed</li>
<li>Referral for treatment of individuals in whom illness symptoms have been assessed.</li>
<li>Nb: application of the nursing process</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="tertiary-prevention">Tertiary prevention<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#tertiary-prevention" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Services aimed at reducing the residual defects that are associated with severe and persistent mental illness.</li>
</ul>
<p><img src="assets/images/image-20251228-17180a3a.jpeg" alt="img-63.jpeg"></p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="focus">Focus:<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#focus" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ol>
<li>Preventing complications of the illness</li>
<li>Promoting rehabilitation that is directed toward achievement of each individuals maximum level of functioning</li>
</ol>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="tertiary-interventions">Tertiary interventions<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#tertiary-interventions" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Consideration of the rehabilitation process at the time of initial diagnosis and treatment planning</li>
<li>Teaching the client daily living skills and encouraging independence to his or her maximum ability</li>
<li>Referring clients for various aftercare services like support groups</li>
</ul>
<p><img src="assets/images/image-20251228-17180a3a.jpeg" alt="img-64.jpeg"></p>
<p>Cont'</p>
<ul>
<li>Monitoring effectiveness of aftercare services</li>
<li>Making referrals for support services when required.</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="settings">Settings<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#settings" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li> Inpatient setups</li>
<li> Out patient departments</li>
<li> Home based care</li>
<li> Group homes</li>
<li> Nursing homes</li>
<li> Community mental health centers.</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="summary">Summary<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#summary" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Prevent</li>
<li>Control</li>
<li>Rehabilitate</li>
</ul>

                                    <span> [X] min</span>
                                    <span> [X] sections</span>
                                </div>
                            </div>
                            <div class="card-arrow"></div>
                        </a>
                        
                        <!-- Topic Card 3 -->
                        <a href="topics/topic-03.html" class="topic-card">
                            <div class="card-number">03</div>
                            <div class="card-content">
                                <h3 class="card-title">[TOPIC 3 TITLE]</h3>
                                <p class="card-description">[Brief description of topic content]</p>
                                <div class="card-meta">
                                    <span> [X] min</span>
                                    <span> [X] sections</span>
                                </div>
                            </div>
                            <div class="card-arrow"></div>
                        </a>
                        
                        <!-- Add more topic cards as needed -->
                        <!-- Copy the topic-card block and update number, href, title, description -->
                        
                    </div>
                </section>

            </main>
        </div>
    </div>

    <script>
        // Theme toggle functionality
        const themeToggle = document.getElementById('theme-toggle');
        const html = document.documentElement;
        
        themeToggle.addEventListener('click', () => {
            const currentTheme = html.getAttribute('data-theme');
            const newTheme = currentTheme === 'light' ? 'dark' : 'light';
            
            html.setAttribute('data-theme', newTheme);
            localStorage.setItem('theme', newTheme);
        });
        
        // Load saved theme
        const savedTheme = localStorage.getItem('theme') || 'light';
        html.setAttribute('data-theme', savedTheme);
    </script>
</body>
</html>

# PDF to HTML Conversion System Prompt (v9.4.4) - Rich UI Edition

**Version:** 9.4.4  
**Last Updated:** December 25, 2025  
**Focus:** Modern UI/UX patterns with 100% content fidelity, nested lists, mathematical equations, and comprehensive interactive quiz system

---

## Overview

This is the comprehensive **PDF to HTML Conversion System Prompt - Rich UI Edition**, featuring enhanced content organization patterns, advanced UI components, mathematical equations support, interactive quiz system, and modern design systems while maintaining absolute content fidelity.

## Core Mission

Convert PDF documents into **visually stunning, accessible, and pedagogically effective** HTML pages while ensuring **100% VERBATIM content preservation**. Create highly appealing and effective learning materials with **modern UI/UX patterns**, organized into **logically coherent chunks**, that maintain absolute fidelity to the original text content with interactive quizzes to reinforce learning and assess comprehension.

---

## Image Handling & Lightbox

All images must be wrapped in a `content-figure` container with the `data-lightbox="true"` attribute to enable the click-to-zoom functionality.

### Image Source Reference

**IMPORTANT**: Use the **exact image filenames** as they appear in `content_cleaned.txt`. Do NOT rename or map images.

#### Image Usage Instructions
1. **Check `content_cleaned.txt`** for image references like:
   ```html
   <img src="assets/images/image-20251225-9d805e34.jpeg" alt="img-1.jpeg">
   ```
2. **Path Resolution Rule**: Use the correct relative path based on the HTML file's location:
   - **Files in `topics/` directory**: Use `../assets/images/`
   - **Files in root directory** (e.g., `index.html`, `comprehensive-exam.html`): Use `assets/images/`
3. **Do NOT rename** images from their timestamp format
4. **Do NOT use** numbered formats like `img-1.jpeg` - use the actual filename

### HTML Structure for Images

```html
<div class="content-figure" data-lightbox="true">
    <div class="figure-image-wrapper">
        <img src="../assets/images/image-20251225-9d805e34.jpeg" alt="[Alt Text]" class="figure-image">
        <div class="figure-overlay">
            <span class="overlay-icon"></span>
            <span class="overlay-text">Click to zoom</span>
        </div>
    </div>
    <p class="figure-caption">Fig. [X.Y]: [Caption Text]</p>
</div>
```

### Image Path Examples

```html
<!-- Correct: Use exact filenames from content_cleaned.txt -->
<img src="../assets/images/image-20251225-9d805e34.jpeg" alt="Gingivitis showing inflamed gums">
<img src="../assets/images/image-20251225-b2c235cf.jpeg" alt="Fibre-optic Endoscope">
<img src="../assets/images/image-20251225-f38697c2.jpeg" alt="Periodontitis diagram">

<!-- Incorrect: Don't use simplified numbered format -->
<img src="../assets/images/img-1.jpeg" alt="...">
<img src="../assets/images/img-12.jpeg" alt="...">
```

---

## Interactive Quiz System

### Quiz System Overview

The quiz system provides 8 different question types to assess learner comprehension. Quizzes are stored in JSON format with versioning support, rendered dynamically via JavaScript, and fully integrated with the existing Rich UI design system.

### Quiz Question Types

#### 1. Multiple Choice (Single Answer)
Standard single-answer questions with 2-6 options.
- **Use Case**: Testing recall of specific facts, definitions, concepts
- **Features**: Radio button selection, immediate feedback, explanation display

#### 2. Multiple Select (Multiple Correct Answers)
Questions where learners select all correct answers.
- **Use Case**: Testing comprehensive understanding of related concepts
- **Features**: Checkbox selection, partial credit option, "Select all that apply" indicator

#### 3. True/False
Binary choice questions for quick knowledge checks.
- **Use Case**: Verifying understanding of statements, common misconceptions
- **Features**: Two-option format, confidence indicator option

#### 4. Fill in the Blank
Text input questions with exact or fuzzy matching.
- **Use Case**: Testing terminology, formulas, key terms
- **Features**: Case-insensitive matching, multiple acceptable answers, hint system
- **CRITICAL**: Question text MUST include `__id__` placeholders (e.g., `__b1__`, `__b2__`) where input fields should appear
- **Example**: `"The liver converts ammonia into __b1__."` with blank ID `"b1"`

#### 5. Matching
Pair items from two columns (drag-and-drop or dropdown).
- **Use Case**: Testing relationships, associations, categorization
- **Features**: Drag-and-drop interface, dropdown fallback, visual feedback

#### 6. Ordering/Sequencing
Arrange items in correct order.
- **Use Case**: Testing processes, procedures, chronological events
- **Features**: Drag-and-drop reordering with live sorting, numbered positions, step validation
- **Implementation Note**: Use "live" sorting during `dragover` events for robust behavior across all environments (including local `file://` protocol).

#### 7. Short Answer
Free-text response with keyword matching.
- **Use Case**: Testing deeper understanding, explanations
- **Features**: Keyword detection, partial credit, model answer display

#### 8. Image-Based Questions
Questions involving image interaction (hotspots, labeling).
- **Use Case**: Anatomy, diagrams, visual identification
- **Features**: Clickable regions, label placement, image zoom

### Media Support (Optional)

Every question can optionally include media (image, video, audio, YouTube) and answer options can optionally include images. All media fields are **optional** - questions work perfectly with text only.

#### Supported Media Types
| Type | Description | Use Case |
|------|-------------|----------|
| `image` | Static image file | Diagrams, photos, charts |
| `video` | Video file (mp4, webm) | Demonstrations, procedures |
| `audio` | Audio file (mp3, wav) | Pronunciation, sounds |
| `youtube` | YouTube embed | Educational videos |

#### Image Answer Options
For multiple-choice and multiple-select questions, each option can optionally include an image. This is useful for visual identification questions where learners select from images rather than text.

####  CRITICAL: Quiz Media Path Resolution
Image and media paths in quiz data files MUST be relative to the **HTML file** that will host the quiz.
- If the quiz is hosted in a file within `topics/` (e.g., `topics/topic-01.html`), use `../assets/images/`.
- If the quiz is hosted in a file in the **root** (e.g., `comprehensive-exam.html`), use `assets/images/`.

### Quiz JSON Schema (v1.0)

Store quiz data in `quizzes/` directory with the following structure:

```
project-name/
 quizzes/
    quiz-schema.json          # Schema definition
    topic-01-quiz.json        # Quiz for topic 01
    topic-02-quiz.json        # Quiz for topic 02
    ...
```

#### Complete Quiz JSON Schema

```json
{
  "$schema": "http://json-schema.org/draft-07/schema#",
  "title": "Quiz Schema v1.0",
  "type": "object",
  "required": ["schemaVersion", "quizId", "metadata", "questions"],
  "properties": {
    "schemaVersion": {
      "type": "string",
      "description": "Schema version for compatibility",
      "pattern": "^\\d+\\.\\d+$",
      "example": "1.0"
    },
    "quizId": {
      "type": "string",
      "description": "Unique identifier for the quiz",
      "pattern": "^[a-z0-9-]+$"
    },
    "metadata": {
      "type": "object",
      "required": ["title", "topicId", "createdAt"],
      "properties": {
        "title": { "type": "string" },
        "description": { "type": "string" },
        "topicId": { "type": "string" },
        "difficulty": { "enum": ["beginner", "intermediate", "advanced"] },
        "estimatedTime": { "type": "integer", "description": "Minutes" },
        "passingScore": { "type": "integer", "minimum": 0, "maximum": 100 },
        "createdAt": { "type": "string", "format": "date-time" },
        "updatedAt": { "type": "string", "format": "date-time" },
        "tags": { "type": "array", "items": { "type": "string" } }
      }
    },
    "settings": {
      "type": "object",
      "properties": {
        "shuffleQuestions": { "type": "boolean", "default": false },
        "shuffleOptions": { "type": "boolean", "default": false },
        "showFeedback": { "enum": ["immediate", "end", "never"], "default": "immediate" },
        "allowRetry": { "type": "boolean", "default": true },
        "showCorrectAnswers": { "type": "boolean", "default": true },
        "timeLimit": { "type": "integer", "description": "Seconds, 0 for unlimited" }
      }
    },
    "questions": {
      "type": "array",
      "items": { "$ref": "#/definitions/question" }
    }
  }
}
```

#### Question Type Definitions

```json
{
  "definitions": {
    "question": {
      "type": "object",
      "required": ["id", "type", "question", "points"],
      "properties": {
        "id": { "type": "string" },
        "type": {
          "enum": [
            "multiple-choice",
            "multiple-select",
            "true-false",
            "fill-blank",
            "matching",
            "ordering",
            "short-answer",
            "image-based"
          ]
        },
        "question": { "type": "string" },
        "points": { "type": "integer", "minimum": 1 },
        "hint": { "type": "string", "description": "OPTIONAL: Hint for the question" },
        "explanation": { "type": "string", "description": "OPTIONAL: Explanation shown after answering" },
        "media": {
          "type": "object",
          "description": "OPTIONAL: Media attachment for the question",
          "properties": {
            "type": { "enum": ["image", "video", "audio", "youtube"] },
            "url": { "type": "string", "description": "URL to media file" },
            "alt": { "type": "string", "description": "Alt text for accessibility" },
            "caption": { "type": "string", "description": "OPTIONAL: Caption below media" },
            "mimeType": { "type": "string", "description": "OPTIONAL: MIME type for video/audio" },
            "videoId": { "type": "string", "description": "YouTube video ID (for youtube type)" },
            "startTime": { "type": "integer", "description": "OPTIONAL: Start time in seconds (youtube)" },
            "autoplay": { "type": "boolean", "default": false },
            "loop": { "type": "boolean", "default": false },
            "muted": { "type": "boolean", "default": false }
          }
        }
      },
      "allOf": [
        {
          "if": { "properties": { "type": { "const": "multiple-choice" } } },
          "then": {
            "properties": {
              "options": {
                "type": "array",
                "minItems": 2,
                "maxItems": 6,
                "items": {
                  "type": "object",
                  "required": ["id", "isCorrect"],
                  "properties": {
                    "id": { "type": "string" },
                    "text": { "type": "string", "description": "Text label (OPTIONAL if image provided)" },
                    "isCorrect": { "type": "boolean" },
                    "image": {
                      "type": "object",
                      "description": "OPTIONAL: Image for this option",
                      "properties": {
                        "url": { "type": "string" },
                        "alt": { "type": "string" }
                      }
                    }
                  }
                }
              }
            }
          }
        },
        {
          "if": { "properties": { "type": { "const": "multiple-select" } } },
          "then": {
            "properties": {
              "options": {
                "type": "array",
                "items": {
                  "type": "object",
                  "required": ["id", "isCorrect"],
                  "properties": {
                    "id": { "type": "string" },
                    "text": { "type": "string", "description": "Text label (OPTIONAL if image provided)" },
                    "isCorrect": { "type": "boolean" },
                    "image": {
                      "type": "object",
                      "description": "OPTIONAL: Image for this option",
                      "properties": {
                        "url": { "type": "string" },
                        "alt": { "type": "string" }
                      }
                    }
                  }
                }
              },
              "partialCredit": { "type": "boolean", "default": true }
            }
          }
        },
        {
          "if": { "properties": { "type": { "const": "true-false" } } },
          "then": {
            "properties": {
              "correctAnswer": { "type": "boolean" }
            }
          }
        },
        {
          "if": { "properties": { "type": { "const": "fill-blank" } } },
          "then": {
            "description": " CRITICAL: The 'question' field MUST contain __id__ placeholders (e.g., __b1__, __b2__) that match the blank IDs. Example: 'The liver converts ammonia into __b1__.' with blank id='b1'",
            "properties": {
              "blanks": {
                "type": "array",
                "description": "Array of blank definitions. Each blank.id must have a matching __id__ placeholder in the question text.",
                "items": {
                  "type": "object",
                  "properties": {
                    "id": { "type": "string", "description": "Blank identifier (e.g., 'b1', '1', 'answer1'). Must match placeholder in question." },
                    "acceptedAnswers": { "type": "array", "items": { "type": "string" }, "description": "List of acceptable answers" },
                    "caseSensitive": { "type": "boolean", "default": false }
                  }
                }
              }
            }
          }
        },
        {
          "if": { "properties": { "type": { "const": "matching" } } },
          "then": {
            "properties": {
              "pairs": {
                "type": "array",
                "items": {
                  "type": "object",
                  "properties": {
                    "id": { "type": "string" },
                    "left": { "type": "string" },
                    "right": { "type": "string" }
                  }
                }
              }
            }
          }
        },
        {
          "if": { "properties": { "type": { "const": "ordering" } } },
          "then": {
            "properties": {
              "items": {
                "type": "array",
                "items": {
                  "type": "object",
                  "properties": {
                    "id": { "type": "string" },
                    "text": { "type": "string" },
                    "correctPosition": { "type": "integer" }
                  }
                }
              }
            }
          }
        },
        {
          "if": { "properties": { "type": { "const": "short-answer" } } },
          "then": {
            "properties": {
              "keywords": { "type": "array", "items": { "type": "string" } },
              "minKeywords": { "type": "integer" },
              "modelAnswer": { "type": "string" },
              "maxLength": { "type": "integer" }
            }
          }
        },
        {
          "if": { "properties": { "type": { "const": "image-based" } } },
          "then": {
            "properties": {
              "imageUrl": { "type": "string" },
              "imageAlt": { "type": "string" },
              "hotspots": {
                "type": "array",
                "items": {
                  "type": "object",
                  "properties": {
                    "id": { "type": "string" },
                    "x": { "type": "number" },
                    "y": { "type": "number" },
                    "radius": { "type": "number" },
                    "label": { "type": "string" },
                    "isCorrect": { "type": "boolean" }
                  }
                }
              },
              "options": {
                "type": "array",
                "description": "OPTIONAL: Alternative to hotspots for multiple-choice style image questions",
                "items": {
                  "type": "object",
                  "required": ["id", "isCorrect"],
                  "properties": {
                    "id": { "type": "string" },
                    "text": { "type": "string" },
                    "isCorrect": { "type": "boolean" }
                  }
                }
              }
            }
          }
        }
      ]
    }
  }
}
```

### Example Quiz JSON Files

#### Example 1: Basic Text Questions (No Media)

```json
{
  "schemaVersion": "1.0",
  "quizId": "pharmacology-intro-quiz",
  "metadata": {
    "title": "Introduction to Pharmacology Quiz",
    "description": "Test your understanding of basic pharmacology concepts",
    "topicId": "topic-01-introduction",
    "difficulty": "beginner",
    "estimatedTime": 10,
    "passingScore": 70,
    "createdAt": "2025-12-24T00:00:00Z",
    "tags": ["pharmacology", "basics", "introduction"]
  },
  "settings": {
    "shuffleQuestions": false,
    "shuffleOptions": true,
    "showFeedback": "immediate",
    "allowRetry": true,
    "showCorrectAnswers": true
  },
  "questions": [
    {
      "id": "q1",
      "type": "multiple-choice",
      "question": "What is the primary function of pharmacokinetics?",
      "points": 10,
      "options": [
        { "id": "a", "text": "Study of drug effects on the body", "isCorrect": false },
        { "id": "b", "text": "Study of how the body processes drugs", "isCorrect": true },
        { "id": "c", "text": "Study of drug interactions", "isCorrect": false },
        { "id": "d", "text": "Study of drug manufacturing", "isCorrect": false }
      ],
      "explanation": "Pharmacokinetics studies ADME: Absorption, Distribution, Metabolism, and Excretion - how the body handles drugs.",
      "hint": "Think about what happens to a drug after you take it."
    },
    {
      "id": "q2",
      "type": "true-false",
      "question": "The therapeutic index is the ratio of the toxic dose to the effective dose.",
      "points": 5,
      "correctAnswer": true,
      "explanation": "TI = TD50/ED50. A higher therapeutic index indicates a safer drug."
    }
  ]
}
```
